   $(document).ready(function () {
	//category dropdown functionality
	$(".popmenu ul li").css('display', 'none');
	$(".byCat ul li").slice(0, 10).css('display', 'block');
	$(".byCat .hide").append('&lt;p id="category_viewall_page_link" class="all"&gt;view all&lt;/p&gt;');
	$(".byLoc ul li").slice(0, 10).css('display', 'block');
	$(".byLoc .hide").append('&lt;p id="location_viewall_page_link" class="all"&gt;view all&lt;/p&gt;');
	$(".byGrp ul li").slice(0, 10).css('display', 'block');
	$(".byGrp .hide").append('&lt;p id="location_category_viewall_page_link" class="all"&gt;view all&lt;/p&gt;');
	$("p.all").click(function () {
		$(this).parent().addClass("all");
		$(this).hide();
		$(this).prev("ul").children("li").css('display', 'block');
	});

    //Mobile Nav dropdown menus
    $(".navLinks").hide();
    $(".toggleNav").toggle(function (){
        $(".navLinks").show()
        .stop();
    }, function(){
        $(".navLinks").hide()
        .stop();
    });

	$(".drop h2").click( function () {
		if ($(this).parent('.drop').hasClass('over')) {
			$(this).parent('.drop').removeClass('over');
	  		$(this).siblings(".hide").stop(true, true).fadeOut(0);
			return false;
		}
		else {
			$(".hide").stop(true, true).fadeOut(0);
			$('.drop').removeClass('over');
			$(this).parent('.drop').addClass("over");
			$(this).siblings(".hide").stop(true, true).fadeIn(0);
			return false;
		}
	});


// Added on 2013-03-04
$(".search label").html("Search Jobs");
/*$('#job_input_text').attr('value', 'Enter keywords, location, or job ID').focus(function () {
	if ($(this).attr('value') == 'Enter keywords, location, or job ID') {
		$(this).attr('value', '');
	}
}).blur(function () {
	if ($(this).attr('value') == '') {
		$(this).attr('value', 'Enter keywords, location, or job ID');
	}
});*/
	
	//Change text in job alerts box
	$('#txtEmail').focus( function() {
		if ($(this).attr('value') == 'Please enter your email address') {
			$(this).attr('value','');	
		}
	}).blur( function() {
		if ($(this).attr('value') == '') {
			$(this).attr('value','Please enter your email address');	
		}
	});
	
	//To fix job descriptions
	if ($('.jobs a').length) {
		$('.jobs a').each( function() {
			var txt = $(this).text();
			$(this).html('');
			var txtArr = txt.split('- ');
			var n = txtArr.length - 1;
			for (var i=0; i&lt;n; i++) {
				$(this).append(txtArr[i]);
			}
			$(this).append('&lt;span class="jobDescLoc"&gt;- '+txtArr[n]+'&lt;/span&gt;');
		});
	}

        //for subscribe button text
        $('#btnSubscribe').attr('value', 'Enter');

	});*/
});

   <script>
    if ("onhashchange" in window) {

      window.onhashchange = function () {
        try {
        
          if (filterResultsEvent) {
          
            filterResultsEvent = false;
            
          } else {
          
            window.location.reload();
            
          }
          
        } catch (e) {
        
          window.location.reload();
          
        }
        
      }
      
    }

    var isEmail = false;

    

    var IsValidCaptcha = false;

    

    function validate_required(field, alerttxt) {

      var address = document.forms['form1'].elements[field].value;
      
      if (address == null || address == "") {
      
        alert(alerttxt);
        
        return false;
        
      } else {
      
        return true;
        
      }
      
    }

    function validate_form(thisform) {

       

        if (window.CandidateCardWidgetEnabled)
            return true;

      if ((document.getElementById("cwuc_jobalertsignupusercontrol_1_hfIsJobAlertRevamp") != null) &amp;&amp; (document.getElementById("cwuc_jobalertsignupusercontrol_1_hfIsJobAlertRevamp").value=="true")) {
              
          return true;

      }

      

      var email = document.getElementById("txtEmail");
      
      if (email != null) {
      
        isEmail = true;
        
      }
      
      if (isEmail) {
      
        with(thisform) {
        
          if (validate_required('txtEmail', "Email address is required") == false) {
            
            document.forms['form1'].elements['txtEmail'].focus();
          
            return false;
            
          }

          if (validateEmail('txtEmail', "Email address is not valid") == false) {
          
            document.forms['form1'].elements['txtEmail'].focus();
            
            return false;
            
          }
          
          
          
          if (document.getElementById("txtCaptcha") != null &amp;&amp; document.getElementById("imgCaptcha") != null) {
          
            refreshCaptcha();  
            IsValidCaptcha = true;
            Show_thickBox();
            return false;
            
          } else if (window.RecaptchaEnabled) {       
          
            
            
            if (window.recaptchaDialogOpen)
            
              return true;
              
            VerifyEmail();
            
            return false;
            
          } else {
            
            return true;
            
          }
          //START BERT_17971

                      
     
        }
        
      } else {
      
        return false;
        
      }
      
    } 

       

    function openPopupWindow(pagename, emailclt) {

      var emailid = document.getElementById(emailclt);
      
      var newPageName = '';
      
      var LocalURL = '';
      
      LocalURL = unescape('?state=rhode+island\u0026category=analytics\u0026dmaid=1950\u0026dmaname=rhode+island'); //BERT19916
      
      // console.log(LocalURL);
      
      if (emailid != null) {
      
        if (LocalURL != null &amp;&amp; LocalURL.length &gt; 0) {
        
          newPageName = '/SubscribeJobs.aspx' + LocalURL + '&amp;email=' + emailid.value;
          
          // console.log(newPageName);
          
        } else {
        
          newPageName = '/SubscribeJobs.aspx?email=' + emailid.value;
          
        }
          
        var retValue = validateEmail(emailclt, 'Email address is required')
        
        if (retValue) {
        
          $.fn.colorbox({
          
            href: newPageName,        
            width: 575,
            height: 580,
            iframe: true,
            overlayClose: false,    
            escKey: false
            
          });
          
        }
        
      }

      return false;
      
    }

    

    function Validatecaptcha() {

      if (document.getElementById("txtCaptcha") != null &amp;&amp; document.getElementById("imgCaptcha") != null &amp;&amp; document.getElementById("TB_ajaxContent") != null) {
      
        var captchaText = null;
        
        var searchEles = document.getElementById("TB_ajaxContent").children;

        if (searchEles.length &gt; 0) {

          for (var i = 0; i &lt; searchEles[0].childNodes.length; i++) {

            if (searchEles[0].childNodes[i].tagName == "INPUT") {
            
              if (searchEles[0].childNodes[i].id == "txtCaptcha") {
              
                captchaText = searchEles[0].childNodes[i].value;
                
                break;
                
              }
              
            }
            
          }
          
        }

        if (captchaText != null &amp;&amp; captchaText != "") {
        
                          
          
          if (document.getElementById("hdnCaptcha") != null) {
          
            document.getElementById("hdnCaptcha").value = captchaText;
            
          }
          
          WebContent.SeoSiteWebContent.ValidateCapatcha(captchaText, onValidateCaptchaSuccess, onValidateCaptchaFailed);
          
        } else {
        
          alert("Please enter valid text");      
          refreshCaptcha();
          return false;
          
        }
        
      }
      
    }

    function onValidateCaptchaSuccess(result) {

      if (result == true) {
      
        if (IsValidCaptcha == false) {
        
          if (document.getElementById("txtEmail") != null &amp;&amp; document.getElementById("txtEmail").value != "") {
          
            Alert.SubscribeAlert.isuserexists(document.getElementById("txtEmail").value, onIsSEOSitesUserExistsSuccess, onIsSEOSitesUserExistsFailed);
            
          } else {
          
            alert('Email address is required');
            
          }
          
        } else if (IsValidCaptcha == true) {
        
          tb_remove();
          
          document.forms["form1"].submit();
          
        } else {
        
          refreshCaptcha();
          
          document.getElementById("txtCaptcha").focus();
          
          return false;
          
        }
        
      } else {
      
        alert("Please enter valid text");
        
        // Reload captcha in case it fails                
        
        refreshCaptcha();
        
        return false;
        
      }
      
    }

    function onValidateCaptchaFailed(result) {

      alert("An error has occured");
      
      return false;
      
    }

    function refreshCaptcha() {

      // Get a reference to CAPTCHA image
      
      var img = document.getElementById("imgCaptcha");
      
      if (img != null &amp;&amp; img != '') {
      
        //Change the image
        
        var newCaptcha = $('#imgCaptcha').attr({
        
          src: '/Handlers/CaptchaImageHandler.ashx' + '?' + (new Date()).getTime()
          
        }).load(function () {
        
          img = newCaptcha;
          
        });
        
        if (document.getElementById("TB_ajaxContent") != null) {
        
          document.getElementById("TB_ajaxContent").innerHTML = document.getElementById("divCaptcha").innerHTML;
          
        }
        
        document.getElementById("txtCaptcha").value = '';
        
      }
      
    }

    // Validate User

    function validateUser() {

      if (document.getElementById("txtEmail") != null &amp;&amp; document.getElementById("txtUserPassword") != null) {
      
        Alert.SubscribeAlert.validateseositeuser(document.getElementById("txtEmail").value, document.getElementById("txtUserPassword").value, onValidateUserSuccess, onValidateUserFailed);
        
      } else {

        // Else? Else what?

      }
      
    }

    function onValidateUserSuccess(result) {

      if (result == null || result.Error != '') {
      
        if (result != null) {
        
          // alert('Password you entered is incorrect.');
          
          if (document.getElementById("pPasswordIncorrect") != null) {
          
            document.getElementById("pPasswordIncorrect").style.display = "block";
            
          }
          
          if (document.getElementById("pSendNewPassword") != null) {
          
            document.getElementById("pSendNewPassword").style.display = "none";
            
          }
          
        }
        
      } else {
      
        if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Error == '') {
        
          if (result.Result == 'PASS') {
          
            $.fn.colorbox.close();
            
            setTimeout("openPopupWindow('/SubscribeJobs.aspx','txtEmail');", 2000);
            
          }
          
        }
        
      }
      
    }

    function onValidateUserFailed(result) {

      alert(result.Error);
      
    }

    function CloseOpenLightBox() {

      $.fn.colorbox.close();
      
    }

    function UserForgotPassword() {

      if (document.getElementById("txtEmail") != null) {
      
        Alert.SubscribeAlert.forgotpassword(document.getElementById("txtEmail").value, onForgotPasswordSuccess, onForgotPasswordFailed);
        
        return false;
        
      } else {

        // Else? Else what?

      }

      return false;
      
    }

    function onForgotPasswordSuccess(result) {

      if (result == null || result.Error != '') {
      
        if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Error == '') {
        
          if (result.Result == '#PASS#') {

            // alert('A new password has been sent to your email address');
            
            if (document.getElementById("pPasswordIncorrect") != null) {
            
              document.getElementById("pPasswordIncorrect").style.display = "none";
              
            }
            
            if (document.getElementById("pSendNewPassword") != null) {
            
              document.getElementById("pSendNewPassword").style.display = "block";
              
            }
            
          }
          
        }
        
      } else {
      
        if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Error == '') {
        
          if (result.Result == '#PASS#') {
          
            // alert('A new password has been sent to your email address');
            
            if (document.getElementById("pPasswordIncorrect") != null) {
            
              document.getElementById("pPasswordIncorrect").style.display = "none";
              
            }
            
            if (document.getElementById("pSendNewPassword") != null) {
            
              document.getElementById("pSendNewPassword").style.display = "block";
              
            }
            
            return false;
            
          }
          
        }
        
      }
      
      return false;
      
    }

    function onForgotPasswordFailed(result) {

      alert(result.Error);
      
    }

    function HidePasswordMessage() {

      if (document.getElementById("pPasswordIncorrect") != null) {
      
        document.getElementById("pPasswordIncorrect").style.display = "none";
        
      }
      
      if (document.getElementById("pSendNewPassword") != null) {
      
        document.getElementById("pSendNewPassword").style.display = "none";
        
      }
      
    }

    function IsSEOSitesUserExists() {

      HidePasswordMessage();
      
      if (validate_required('txtEmail', "Email address is required") == false) {
      
        document.forms['form1'].elements['txtEmail'].focus();
        
        return false;
        
      }
      
      var retValue = validateEmail('txtEmail', 'Email address is not valid');
      
      if (!retValue) {
      
        return false;
        
      }
      
      if (document.getElementById("txtEmail") != null) {
      
        
        
        if (document.getElementById("txtCaptcha") != null &amp;&amp; document.getElementById("imgCaptcha") != null) {
        
          refreshCaptcha();     
          IsValidCaptcha = false;
          Show_thickBox();
          
        } else {
        
          Alert.SubscribeAlert.isuserexists(document.getElementById("txtEmail").value, onIsSEOSitesUserExistsSuccess, onIsSEOSitesUserExistsFailed);
          
        }              
        
      }
      
    }

    function onIsSEOSitesUserExistsSuccess(result) {

      
      
      if (document.getElementById("txtCaptcha") != null &amp;&amp; document.getElementById("imgCaptcha") != null &amp;&amp; document.getElementById("TB_ajaxContent") != null) {
      
        tb_remove();
        
      }
      
      if (result == null || result.Error != '') {
      
        if (result != null) {
        
          $.fn.colorbox.close();
          
          openPopupWindow('/SubscribeJobs.aspx', 'txtEmail');
          
        }
        
      } else {
      
        if (result != null) {
        
          if (result.Result == 'TRUE') {
          
            
            
            document.getElementById("txtUserPassword").value = "";
            
            
            
            $("#cboxOverlay").show();
            
            $.colorbox.resize();
            
            $.fn.colorbox({
            
              width: "575px",
              inline: true,
              href: "#inline_Password",
              onComplete: function () {
              
                $('#txtUserPassword').focus();
                
              }
              
            });
            
          }
          
        }
        
      }
      
    }

    function onIsSEOSitesUserExistsFailed(result) {

      alert(result.Error);
      
    }

    

    function setJAConfirmationPopup(minutes, seconds, Message) {
    
        var objDate = new Date();

        var secondsLocal = objDate.getSeconds();

        var minutesLocal = objDate.getMinutes();

        if (minutesLocal == minutes) {

            if (secondsLocal &gt; seconds &amp;&amp; secondsLocal - seconds &lt; 15) {
    
                alert(Message);
      
            }
    
        } else if (minutesLocal == parseInt(minutes) + 1) {

            secondsLocal = secondsLocal + 60;
    
            if (secondsLocal &gt; seconds &amp;&amp; secondsLocal - seconds &lt; 15) {

                alert(Message);
      
            }
    
        }

    } // setJAConfirmationPopup

    

    function VerifyEmail() {

      Alert.SubscribeAlert.verifyEmail(document.getElementById("txtEmail").value, onVerifyEmailSuccess, onVerifyEmailFail);
      
    }

    function onVerifyEmailSuccess(result) {

      if (parseInt(result.Result, 10) % 2 == 0) {
      
        var emailVerificationCode = document.getElementById('emailVerificationCode');
        
        if (emailVerificationCode)
        
          emailVerificationCode.value = result.Result;
          
        if (window.ResponsiveEnabled)
        
          openJobAlertsForm('txtEmail', unescape('?state=rhode+island\u0026category=analytics\u0026dmaid=1950\u0026dmaname=rhode+island')); //BERT19916
          
        else if (window.RecaptchaEnabled)
        
          showRecaptchaDialog();
          
        else
        
          IsSEOSitesUserExists();
          
      } else {

        alert('Please enter a valid email address.');
        
        document.getElementById("txtEmail").value = "";
        
      }
      
    }

    function onVerifyEmailFail(result) {

      alert(result.Error);
      
    }

        $('#fade , .popup_block').fadeOut(function () {

      });

          $('#fade, a.close').remove();
          
        }); //fade them both out

          $('#fade, a.close').remove();

      });

      $('.400limit').keyup(function () {
      
        var len = this.value.length;
        
        if (len &gt;= 400) {
        
          this.value = this.value.substring(0, 400);
          
        }
        
        // $('#charLeft').text(150 - len);
        
      });

      $('.150limit').keyup(function () {
      
        var len = this.value.length;
        
        if (len &gt;= 150) {
        
          this.value = this.value.substring(0, 150);
          
        }
        
      });
      
    });

    

    function ShowDiv(divId) {

      var popID = divId;
      
      var popWidth = 450; //Gets the first query string value
      
      // Fade in the Popup and add close button
      
      $('#' + popID).fadeIn().css({
      
        'width': Number(popWidth)
        
      }); //.prepend('&lt;a href="#" class="close"&gt;&lt;img src="images/admin/popupClose.gif" class="btn_close" alt="Close" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;');        
      
      // Define margin for center alignment (vertical + horizontal) - we add 80 to the height/width to accomodate for the padding + border width defined in the css
      
      var popMargTop = ($('#' + popID).height() + 80) / 2;
      
      var popMargLeft = ($('#' + popID).width() + 80) / 2;
      
      // Apply Margin to Popup
      
      $('#' + popID).css({
      
        'margin-top': -popMargTop,
        
        'margin-left': -popMargLeft
        
      });
      
      $('body').append('&lt;div id="fade"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;'); // Add the fade layer to bottom of the body tag.
      
      $('#fade').css({
      
        'filter': 'alpha(opacity=80)'
        
      }).fadeIn(); //Fade in the fade layer 
      
    }

    function ShowDivNew(divId) {

      var popWidth = 450; //Gets the first query string value
      
      // Fade in the Popup and add close button
      
      divId.fadeIn().css({
      
        'width': Number(popWidth)
        
      }).prepend('&lt;a href="#" class="close"&gt;&lt;img src="images/admin/popupClose.gif" class="btn_close" alt="Close" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;');
      
      // Define margin for center alignment (vertical + horizontal) - we add 80 to the height/width to accomodate for the padding + border width defined in the css
      
      var popMargTop = (divId.height() + 80) / 2;
      
      var popMargLeft = (divId.width() + 80) / 2;
      
      // Apply Margin to Popup
      
      divId.css({
      
        'margin-top': -popMargTop,
        
        'margin-left': -popMargLeft
        
      });
      
      $('body').append('&lt;div id="fade"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;'); //Add the fade layer to bottom of the body tag.
      
      $('#fade').css({
      
        'filter': 'alpha(opacity=80)'
        
      }).fadeIn(); //Fade in the fade layer
      
    }

    

    function AddEmailEvents() {

      var email = document.getElementById("txtEmail");
      
      if (email != null) {
      
        email.onfocus = function () {
        
          isEmail = true;
          
        }
        
        email.onblur = function () {
        
          isEmail = false;
          
        }
        
      }

      var bt = document.getElementById("btnSubscribe");
      
      if (bt != null) {
      
        bt.onfocus = function () {
        
          isEmail = true;
          
        }
        
        bt.onblur = function () {
        
          isEmail = false;
          
        }
        
      }
      
    }

function AddFilterSettings() {

        var URL = document.location.toString();
        var FilterUrl =getCookie("FilterUrl");

        //BERT 21260 STARTS
       var BasicURL='';

       // undefined check for IE8
      if ((! typeof FilterUrl == undefined) &amp;&amp; FilterUrl.match('#')){

       BasicURL=FilterUrl.split('#')[0];
         
       if( BasicURL == URL) {
        //BERT 21260 ENDS

        var anchor = FilterUrl.split('#')[1];
        
        document.getElementById('jobTitleKeyword').value = anchor.split('/')[0];
        
        document.getElementById('locationsKeyword').value = (anchor.split('/').length &gt; 0) ? anchor.split('/')[1] : '';
        
        
        
        if (document.getElementById('dateKeyword') != null) {
        
          document.getElementById('dateKeyword').value = (anchor.split('/').length &gt; 0) ? anchor.split('/')[2] : '';
          
        }
        
        
        
        if (document.getElementById('categoryKeyword') != null) {
        
          document.getElementById('categoryKeyword').value = (anchor.split('/').length &gt; 0) ? anchor.split('/')[2] : '';
          
        }

        eval(document.getElementById("btGo").href.replace('javascript:', '').replace(/%20/g, ' '));
        
      }
      
     }

    }

    function OnGoFilter(url, isSearchPaging, isDate) {

      

      //BERT:19723
      
   
//      filterTitle = document.getElementById("hdnFilterTitle").value;
//      
//      filterLocation = document.getElementById("hdnFilterLocation").value;

//      jobTitleKeyword = Trim(document.getElementById("jobTitleKeyword").value);
//      
//      locationKeyword = Trim(document.getElementById("locationsKeyword").value);
//      
//      
//      
//      if (document.getElementById("dateKeyword") != null) {
//      
//        dateKeyword = Trim(document.getElementById("dateKeyword").value);
//        
//        document.location.href = document.location.toString().split('#')[0] + '#' + jobTitleKeyword + '/' + locationKeyword + '/' + dateKeyword;
//        
//      } else if (document.getElementById("categoryKeyword") != null) { //BERT 4356. Display filter by category control based on the template
//        
//        categoryKeyword = Trim(document.getElementById("categoryKeyword").value);
//        
//        document.location.href = document.location.toString().split('#')[0] + '#' + jobTitleKeyword + '/' + locationKeyword + '/' + categoryKeyword;
//        
//      } else if ((jobTitleKeyword != '' &amp;&amp; jobTitleKeyword != filterTitle) || (locationKeyword != '' &amp;&amp; locationKeyword != filterLocation)) {

//        
//      
//        document.location.href = document.location.toString().split('#')[0] + '#' + jobTitleKeyword + '/' + locationKeyword;
//        
//      }

      var FilterUrl='';

      $("#hdnPageNationId")[0].value="1";

      filterTitle = document.getElementById("hdnFilterTitle").value;
      
      filterLocation = document.getElementById("hdnFilterLocation").value;

      if (document.getElementById("jobTitleKeyword") != null) {
        jobTitleKeyword = Trim(document.getElementById("jobTitleKeyword").value);
      }
      else{
        jobTitleKeyword=filterTitle;
      }

      if (document.getElementById("locationsKeyword") != null) {
        locationKeyword = Trim(document.getElementById("locationsKeyword").value);
      }
      else{
        locationKeyword=filterLocation;
      }

      
      
      if (document.getElementById("dateKeyword") != null) {
      
        dateKeyword = Trim(document.getElementById("dateKeyword").value);
        FilterUrl = document.location.toString().split('#')[0] + '#' + jobTitleKeyword + '/' + locationKeyword + '/' + dateKeyword;
        
      } else if (document.getElementById("categoryKeyword") != null) { //BERT 4356. Display filter by category control based on the template
        
        categoryKeyword = Trim(document.getElementById("categoryKeyword").value);
        FilterUrl = document.location.toString().split('#')[0] + '#' + jobTitleKeyword + '/' + locationKeyword + '/' + categoryKeyword;
        
      } else if ((jobTitleKeyword != '' &amp;&amp; jobTitleKeyword != filterTitle) || (locationKeyword != '' &amp;&amp; locationKeyword != filterLocation)) {

        
        FilterUrl = document.location.toString().split('#')[0] + '#' + jobTitleKeyword + '/' + locationKeyword;
        
      }
      setFilterCookie("FilterUrl", FilterUrl);//BERT 21260

      //BERT:19723
      
      
      
      url = url.replace(/&#39;+/g, '%27');
      
      
      
      url = url.replace(/&#232;+/g, '');
      
      url = url.replace(/&#233;+/g, '');
      
      url = url.replace(/&#224;+/g, '');
      
      url = url.replace(/&#225;+/g, '');
      
      Go(url, isSearchPaging, isDate);
      
    }

  
    function Trim(str) {

      str = str.replace('\\s+', ' ');
      
      str = str.replace(/(^\s+)|(\s+$)/g, '');
      
      return str;
      
    }

    
    function refreshCaptcha() {

      // Get a reference to CAPTCHA image
      
      var img = document.getElementById("imgCaptcha");
      
      if (img != null &amp;&amp; img != '') {
      
        //Change the image
        
        var newCaptcha = $('#imgCaptcha').attr({
        
          src: '/Handlers/CaptchaImageHandler.ashx' + '?' + (new Date()).getTime()
          
        }).load(function () {
        
          img = newCaptcha;
          
        });
        
        if (document.getElementById("TB_ajaxContent") != null) {
        
          document.getElementById("TB_ajaxContent").innerHTML = document.getElementById("divCaptcha").innerHTML;
          
        }
        
        document.getElementById("txtCaptcha").value = '';
        
        
        
        $("#TB_window input:first").blur().focus().focus();
        
      }
      
    }

    

    $(document).ready(

      function () {
      
        try {
          var pageNationId = $("#hdnPageNationId")[0].value;
          
          if (pageNationId != "0" &amp;&amp; pageNationId != "" &amp;&amp; pageNationId != "1" &amp;&amp; pageNationId != "undefined") {
          
            // Get the requested URL without paramaters
            
            var url = ($("#jobs_next_page_link")[0].href.split('(')[1].split(','))[0];
            
            $("#hdnPageNationId")[0].value = pageNationId;

            url = url.replace(/\'/g,'');
            
            Paging(url, pageNationId, "true", "true");
            
          }

          $("#jobs_next_page_link").live("click", function (obj) {        

              if(obj.currentTarget.href.split(',').length&gt;1){ 

                   $("#hdnPageNationId")[0].value = obj.currentTarget.href.split(',')[1].replace(/\'/g,'').replace(/\ /g,'')
             
              } else {
                  
                  $("#hdnPageNationId")[0].value = obj.currentTarget.innerHTML.replace(/\ /g, "");
              
              }
            
            return true;
            
          });
          
        } catch (e) {}
        
      });
